# <a name="analytic-trace-event-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd9b2-102">Çözümleme İzleme Etkinliği Başvurusu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd9b2-102">Analytic Trace Event Reference</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="dd9b2-103">Aşağıdaki tabloda tanımlayıcıları olay düzeyleri tanımlar ve iletileri ilişkili [!INCLUDE[indigo2](../../../../../includes/indigo2-md.md)] analitik izleme.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd9b2-103">The following table defines the event levels, identifiers, and messages associated with the [!INCLUDE[indigo2](../../../../../includes/indigo2-md.md)] Analytic Tracing.</span></span>
